< Review>
i am a on the fence about  recommending to go with AQS. I will say they are awesome at customer service. Their service managers (Elinore who has helped me) is top notch. and the installer (Rene) is great at his job.
Now to my experience and as to why i dont know whether to recommend or not to.
With the initial visit(THE QUOTE): the sales people were really cool and really good at their pitch. The one thing i would say is to make sure you know exactly what you are getting before they leave. i was quoted a price for a Rheem unit. Thinking i was getting a Rheem unit as promised i waited to see what was done after it was all installed.  I noticed they installed a RUUD unit. I called to express my concern and got the whole, RHEEM makes RUUD so its basically the same thing answer. so i feel i got charged for a RHEEM but got a RUUD. (OVERCHARGED)
The installation has not gone as smooth as i thought it was going to be. (maybe i was just the lucky one for all the problems to happen to).  Although all the issues that have came up after the install have been addressed and taken care of in a quick manner.
So overall, the air conditioner is working great and doing what it is supposed to do. All i can say is if you do decide to go with AQS, i just hope you have a better experience than i have had. I dont regret getting the ac unit because we really needed it but i do feel i got had a little bit.</Review>

< review>
It's more than chiropractic care, it's total body care! I have a degenerative disc in my back and two bulging discs in my neck, and that can make it rough sometimes working as a lineman, but these guys keep me going. They have three doctors but I've only seen two, Dr John and Dr James. Using the body scan method they can pinpoint where things are out of alignment and make the necessary corrections with the Activator which makes micro adjustments or they can do a good old fashioned manual adjustment. I usually opt for the Activator, unless I feel the need for a little more and go with a manual or drop table. All the massage therapist are good and have their own unique style. Beau has recently started taping my back which has surprisingly helped. Shanon has a one of a kind massage technique that completely relaxes your body and her hour massage is well worth the price. So there are a lot of options to get your body working and feeling better.lo<//review>

< Text>
This was a lucky turn off the road for me during my drive from Palm Springs to San Diego. It was a nice place to stop for a minute and see what there is to see. A nice walk led you through the desert landscape with plenty of informational placards explaining the indigenous peoples of the area, their lives, histories, and how they exist today. The most interesting part was the information about the singing and the speaker that played 2 different songs. I really enjoyed listening and being there.</Text>

<Rate>5< /Rate><Review>Beautiful little road-side pull-out along the Palms-to-Pines Highway.  I'll mention right away that this parking area has a garbage can to dispose of your travelling trash (that's what I call the small incidental stuff that you generate while on a road trip).  This is a big deal, as I've found here in southern California - there are a few pull-outs that don't provide any garbage disposal, ie: garbage can would be a good start, and travellers just throw their junk around the parking lots.  That's pretty sad, when you're in a scenic overlook, and all you see is garbage blowing around.  Having said that, THIS vista point does have garbage cans, and it's a nice clean area - with some easy walks from the parking area to the vista points.  This was a joy to stop at and stretch our legs, breathe in some really fresh air, and on our way again.< /Review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOWA-OksH84_MYv05_f66tprTeqzE9V6J8IT0H7=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPlzloiMfVLFk_tUD61ezZ_G8FENu45JIITnyLL=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM14RHYW-Wvqwf9QC9WJh8uTSwcApGiA3gwvUdn=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOkwb2pEfXokvO0HwwcIne3l7SZIUsm-b22m_a3=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM9MUaz8FlOVqkCQeBKHMhxem6weRZ1DsY5eBhg=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO7jqBHf9nW0C1NcHeHprKxNiPvVjITCvTl0hTx=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOfNX0bcb7NlhE3RIiDSGc8GLH7MYJDkK0TqcTU=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM3KiX7s_gmRYUCtTEd0Tf9pu1Vqh8JCczE8ap0=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNAZ0F9RPOoMbjmhsAe6thO2AgNgOiFEqgFJDYQ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMfhiIw2cLeTVEAo_cAOSxSGWV60C4IopY7OUpf=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pics><Resp>None<//Resp><gmapID>0x80dbab2e8f2cbc1d:0x1b53ec328310477<//gmapID></record>

1547967607339<//Date>
<Rate>5<//Rate><Text>During some of our roadtrips we purposely like to look for lookouts or view points or lookouts just to look at the areas and learn more about the scenery and area. One of my favorites, which I discover a couple years ago is an area on Hyw 74 in California known as the Palms to Pines Highway. There are actually two view points in the area. The Cochella Valley Vista Point which is the more popular stop and The Cahuilla Tewanet Vista Point.  To us it's important to make these stop because you can find some information about that area.

These were taken at the Cahuilla Tewanet Vista Point. This vista point is great not only for its views but also the information it gives on the Mukat people of the Agua Caliente band of Cahuilla Indians. The views of the beautiful mountains and desert landscape was a wonderful mix. I did a little research on the Cahuilla Indians and it was interesting to find out that they used bird songs to teach their young their language and they called the area of Palm Springs "Sec-he which means "boiling Water".</Text>< pictures>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
Yesterday, I visted this particular location.  I had not been here in about 4 years, so I had lower expectations as quality usually drops.   However, I was ultimately surprised to find the quality of a higher tier.   I did find it a little odd to have Tapatio at a pizza joint, but I was OK with it.  The salad bar was stocked with many different dressings and sauces, but I only picked out ranch for my party's pizza.   I know for sure, that next time, I will try tue thousand island and honey mustard.   I also found the specials and free magnets enjoyable.  However, we should not forget about the main thing; the pizza!   The pizza was quite phenomenal, as it always is at Round Table Pizza locations.   While it was quite greasy and was somewhat problematic when putting parmesan cheese on it, it was still exceptional, perhaps the best of anuly chain restaurant, abd better than many smaller restaurants.  The drinks were also enjoyable.   In the end, Round Table Pizza definitely deserved its perfect score.< /review>
